    <string name="philosophy_text">"&lt;p>SpeedSpot lets you test the speed of internet connections and more importantly it enables you to share your WiFi test results taken in hotels, cafes, restaurants and many other places with the SpeedSpot Community. That also means it enables all SpeedSpotters to share their results with you. This way you can find the fastest WiFi hotspots anywhere in the world. &lt;/p> &lt;p>Speed matters - because video conferencing, streaming movies or music, sharing photos or videos is no fun when you have a poor internet connection. But, due to poor network coverage and mobile carriers installing increasing amounts of data caps, WiFi will still be the most reliable way to do data intensive tasks over the next few years. So why isn't there a way to find fast WiFi hotspots? I don't know either, but I think there should be. That's why I built SpeedSpot.&lt;/p>"</string>

    <string name="privacy_policy_text">&lt;p>This privacy policy governs your use of the software application SpeedSpot (“Application”) for mobile devices that was created by Frederik Lipfert. The Application is a mobile speed test and Wi-Fi finder. With SpeedSpot you can test the speed of cellular and Wi-Fi connections and share information about Wi-Fi hotspots with the SpeedSpot community so SpeedSpot users can find fast Wi-Fi hotspots. &lt;p>&lt;b>What information does the Application obtain and how is it used?&lt;/b>&lt;br> &lt;i>User Provided Information&lt;/i>&lt;br> No registration is required to use the Application. &lt;i>Automatically Collected Information &lt;/i>&lt;br> The Application may collect certain information automatically, including, but not limited to, the type of mobile device you use, your mobile devices unique device ID, the IP address of your mobile device, your mobile operating system, the type of mobile Internet browsers you use, and information about the way you use the Application. &lt;/p> &lt;p>&lt;b>Does the Application collect precise real time location information of the device?&lt;/b>&lt;br> In order to monitor and improve the speed test algorithm all tests taken are stored, but no personal information is collected and therefore none is stored that connects a test to the SpeedSpot User taking it. The anonymous test results include the ping (ms), download &amp; upload speed (Mbps), the IPv4 or IPv6 network address, the test time, connection type (cellular or Wi-Fi), carrier name and SSID, as well as, if you explicitly allowed location access, the approximate location information. For tests that you choose to add to the Wi-Fi Finder database also the name and the venue type (hotel, cafe, etc.) is collected.&lt;br> If you do not want us to use your location for the purposes set forth above, you should turn off the location services for the mobile application located in your account settings or in your mobile phone settings and/or within the mobile application. &lt;/p> &lt;p>&lt;b>Do third parties see and/or have access to information obtained by the Application?&lt;/b>&lt;br> Yes. We will share your information with third parties only in the ways that are described in this privacy statement.&lt;br> We may disclose User Provided and Automatically Collected Information:&lt;br> • as required by law, such as to comply with a subpoena, or similar legal process;&lt;br> • when we believe in good faith that disclosure is necessary to protect our rights, protect your safety or the safety of others, investigate fraud, or respond to a government request;&lt;br> • with our trusted services providers who work on our behalf, do not have an independent use of the information we disclose to them, and have agreed to adhere to the rules set forth in this privacy statement.&lt;br> • if Frederik Lipfert is involved in a merger, acquisition, or sale of all or a portion of its assets, you will be notified via email and/or a prominent notice on our Web site of any change in ownership or uses of this information, as well as any choices you may have regarding this information.&lt;/p> &lt;p>&lt;b>What are my opt-out rights?&lt;/b>&lt;br> You can stop all collection of information by the Application easily by uninstalling the Application. You may use the standard uninstall processes as may be available as part of your mobile device or via the mobile application marketplace or network. &lt;/p> &lt;p>&lt;b>Data Retention Policy, Managing Your Information&lt;/b>&lt;br> We will retain User Provided data for as long as you use the Application and for a reasonable time thereafter. We will retain Automatically Collected anonymous information and thereafter may store it in aggregate. &lt;/p> &lt;p>&lt;b>Children&lt;/b>&lt;br> We do not use the Application to knowingly solicit data from or market to children under the age of 13. If a parent or guardian becomes aware that his or her child has provided us with information without their consent, he or she should contact us at support@speedspot.org. We will delete such information from our files within a reasonable time.&lt;/p> &lt;p>&lt;b>Security&lt;/b>&lt;br> We are concerned about safeguarding the confidentiality of your information. We provide physical, electronic, and procedural safeguards to protect information we process and maintain. For example, we limit access to this information to authorized employees and contractors who need to know that information in order to operate, develop or improve our Application. Please be aware that, although we endeavor provide reasonable security for information we process and maintain, no security system can prevent all potential security breaches.&lt;/p> &lt;p>&lt;b>Changes&lt;/b>&lt;br> This Privacy Policy may be updated from time to time for any reason. We will notify you of any changes to our Privacy Policy by updating the Privacy Policy in the Application. You are advised to consult this Privacy Policy regularly for any changes, as continued use is deemed approval of all changes. &lt;/p> &lt;p>&lt;b>Google Analytics&lt;/b>&lt;br> We use Google Analytics to track the number of active users, from where in the world the application is being used, adoption and usage of specific features and crashes and exceptions. All this data is collected anonymously. &lt;/p> &lt;p>&lt;b>Your Consent&lt;/b>&lt;br> By using the Application, you are consenting to our processing of your information as set forth in this Privacy Policy now and as amended by us. ”Processing”, means using cookies on a computer/hand held device or using or touching information in any way, including, but not limited to, collecting, storing, deleting, using, combining and disclosing information, all of which activities will take place in Germany. If you reside outside Germany your information will be transferred, processed and stored there under German privacy standards.&lt;/p> &lt;p>&lt;b>Contact us&lt;/b>&lt;br> If you have any questions regarding privacy while using the Application, or have questions about our practices, please contact us via email at support@speedspot.org.&lt;/p> &lt;p>Location suggestions are provided by Expedia.&lt;/p></string>
